4796: const renderProgressive = (tbody, data, renderRowFn, chunkSize = 40) => {
4797:   const token=(APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.get(tbody)||0)+1;APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.set(tbody,token);
4798:   tbody.innerHTML = "";
4799:   if (!data || !data.length) return;
4800:   const safeChunkSize = data.length > 5000 ? Math.min(chunkSize, 28) : chunkSize;
4801:   let index = 0;
4802:   const renderNextChunk = () => {
4803:       if(APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.get(tbody)!==token)return;
4804:       const chunk = data.slice(index, index + safeChunkSize);
4805:       if (!chunk.length) return;
4806:       const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
4807:       const temp = document.createElement("tbody");
4808:       temp.innerHTML = chunk.map(renderRowFn).join("");
4809:       while(temp.firstChild) fragment.appendChild(temp.firstChild);
4810:       if(APP_RUNTIME.renderTokens.get(tbody)!==token)return;
4811:       tbody.appendChild(fragment);
4812:       index += safeChunkSize;
4813:       if (index < data.length) scheduleUiWork(renderNextChunk);
4814:   };
4815:   // Render the first chunk immediately so a filter change never leaves the table visually blank.
4816:   // Remaining chunks still use idle/animation scheduling to keep large datasets responsive.
4817:   renderNextChunk();
4818: };

4823:   if (v === null || v === undefined) return "N/A";
4824:   if (v === Infinity) return "∞";
4825:   if (!isFinite(v)) return "N/A"; 
4826:   if (v < 0) return "-" + Math.abs(v*100).toFixed(2) + "%"; 
4827:   return (v*100).toFixed(2)+"%"; 
4828: }

4830: // One global visual rule for actual ACOS values across every module.
4831: // 1%-39% = green; 40%-60% = yellow; >=61% (and Infinity) = red.
4832: const getAcosBand = (v) => {
4833:   if (v === Infinity) return "bad";
4834:   if (!Number.isFinite(v) || v < 0.01) return "neutral";
4835:   if (v >= 0.61) return "bad";
4836:   if (v >= 0.40) return "warn";
4837:   return "good";
4838: };

4842:   return `<span class="acosValue acos-${getAcosBand(v)}" data-acos-value="${v === Infinity ? "Infinity" : escapeHtml(String(v ?? ""))}">${label}${value}</span>`;
4843: };

4852: const safeNum = (x) => { 
4853:   if (typeof x === "number") return isFinite(x) ? x : 0; 
4854:   if (x === null || x === undefined || x === "") return 0; 
4855:   const raw = String(x).trim();
4856:   const negativeByParentheses = /^\(.*\)$/.test(raw);
4857:   const clean = raw.replace(/[£$€¥,%\s,]/g, "").replace(/[()]/g, ""); 
4858:   const n = parseFloat(clean); 
4859:   if (!isFinite(n)) return 0;
4860:   return negativeByParentheses ? -n : n; 
4861: };

4863: const getNumericInput = (id, fallback, min = -Infinity, max = Infinity) => {

4865:   const raw = el?.value;

4868:   return Number.isFinite(parsed) ? clamp(parsed, min, max) : clamp(fallback, min, max);

4871: let asinEconomicsCache = { raw:"", map:new Map(), invalid:[] };
4872: const parseAsinEconomicsOverrides = () => {
4873:   const raw = String($("asinEconomicsInput")?.value || "").trim();
4874:   if (asinEconomicsCache.raw === raw) return asinEconomicsCache;
4875:   const map = new Map(), invalid = [];
4876:   raw.split(/\r?\n/).map(x => x.trim()).filter(Boolean).forEach((line, idx) => {
4877:     const cells = line.split(/[\t,]/).map(x => x.trim());
4878:     if (idx === 0 && /asin/i.test(cells[0] || "") && !/^[A-Z0-9]{10}$/i.test(cells[0] || "")) return;
4879:     const asin = String(cells[0] || "").toUpperCase();

5079: const toISODate = (d) => {
5080:   if (typeof d === "number" && isFinite(d)) { 
5081:     const dateObj = new Date(Math.round((d - 25569) * 86400000)); 
5082:     return `${dateObj.getUTCFullYear()}-${String(dateObj.getUTCMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(dateObj.getUTCDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`; 
5083:   }
5084:   const s = String(d || "").trim();
5085:   if (!s) return "";
5086:   const isoMatch = s.match(/^(\d{4})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})/);
5087:   if (isoMatch) return `${isoMatch[1]}-${isoMatch[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${isoMatch[3].padStart(2,'0')}`;
5088:   const zhMatch = s.match(/^(\d{4})年\s*(\d{1,2})月\s*(\d{1,2})日?/);
5089:   if (zhMatch) return `${zhMatch[1]}-${zhMatch[2].padStart(2,'0')}-${zhMatch[3].padStart(2,'0')}`;
5090:   const euMatch = s.match(/^(\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{1,2})[-\/.](\d{4})/);
5091:   if (euMatch) {
5092:       const p1 = parseInt(euMatch[1], 10), p2 = parseInt(euMatch[2], 10), y = parseInt(euMatch[3], 10);
5093:       let m = p1, day = p2; if (p1 > 12) { day = p1; m = p2; }
5094:       return `${y}-${String(m).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(day).padStart(2,'0')}`;
5095:   }
5096:   const dt = new Date(s); 
5097:   if (!isNaN(dt.getTime())) return `${dt.getFullYear()}-${String(dt.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(dt.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}`;
5098:   return ""; 
5099: };

4324:   if(raw==="US"||raw==="USA"||raw==="AMAZON.COM")return"US";
4325:   if(raw==="CA"||raw==="CANADA"||raw==="AMAZON.CA")return"CA";
4326:   if(raw==="MX"||raw==="MEXICO"||raw==="AMAZON.COM.MX")return"MX";
4327:   return raw;

4338: };

6163: // ==================== SQP Funnel Analysis ====================
6164: const renderSqpAnalysis = () => {
6165:     const tbody = $("sqpTable")?.querySelector("tbody");
6166:     if (!tbody) return;
6167:     if (!AdsStore.sqp.length) {
6168:         tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;color:var(--muted);padding:30px;">${t('dyn_no_sqp')}</td></tr>`;
6169:         return;
6170:     }
6171:     const sorted = [...AdsStore.sqp].sort((a,b) => b.searchVolume - a.searchVolume).slice(0, 50);
6172:     tbody.innerHTML = sorted.map(d => {
6173:         let insight = currentLang === "zh" ? "份额结构相对稳定" : "Share structure relatively stable";
6174:         let insightClass = "good";
6175:         if (d.clickShare < d.imprShare * 0.5) {
6176:             insight = currentLang === "zh" ? "点击份额偏弱：优先检查主图、价格、评分、配送与标题相关性" : "Click share is weak: review image, price, rating, delivery and title relevance";
6177:             insightClass = "bad";
6178:         } else if (d.cartShare < d.clickShare * 0.6) {
6179:             insight = currentLang === "zh" ? "加购份额偏弱：优先检查详情页、变体、优惠与竞品差异" : "Cart share is weak: review detail page, variations, promotion and competitor gap";
6180:             insightClass = "warn";
6181:         } else if (d.purchShare < d.cartShare * 0.7) {
6182:             insight = currentLang === "zh" ? "购买份额偏弱：优先检查价格、Coupon、库存、配送与评价" : "Purchase share is weak: review price, coupon, stock, delivery and reviews";
6183:             insightClass = "bad";
6184:         }
6185:         const meta = [d.asin, d.reportingPeriod || (d.startDate && d.endDate ? `${d.startDate}~${d.endDate}` : "")].filter(Boolean).join(" · ");
6186:         return `<tr title="${escapeHtml(meta)}">
6187:           <td style="font-weight:600; color:var(--text);">${escapeHtml(d.query)}</td>
6188:           <td>${fmtInt(d.searchVolume)}</td><td>${fmtPct(d.imprShare)}</td><td>${fmtPct(d.clickShare)}</td>
6189:           <td>${fmtPct(d.cartShare)}</td><td>${fmtPct(d.purchShare)}</td><td>${fmtPct(d.brandCvr)}</td>
6190:           <td><span class="tag ${insightClass}" style="white-space:normal;line-height:1.35;">${escapeHtml(insight)}</span></td>
6191:         </tr>`;
6192:     }).join("");
6193: };
